class="sticky-inner-wrapper" style="position:relative;top:0px"><div class="Header__component"><div class="Header__wrapper"><div class="Logo__component"><a class="Logo__cnn" href="/" class="Chrome__content"><div class="story"><div class="BasicArticle__component"><div class="Zone__component BasicArticle__zone BasicArticle__series dark"><div class="Zone__wrapper"><div class="BasicArticle__seriesWrapper"><a class="BasicArticle__seriesTitle" href="/specials/world/one-square-meter" target="_blank">One Square Meter</a><a class="BasicArticle__seriesLink" href="/specials/world/one-square-meter" target="_blank">View All</a></div></div></div><div class="Zone__component BasicArticle__zone BasicArticle__head dark"><div class="Zone__wrapper"><div class="PageHead__component"><a class="PageHead__section" aria-current="false" href="/style/architecture">architecture</a><h1 class="PageHead__title">Shanghai Tower unveils world&#x27;s highest art space</h1><div class="PageHead__published">Updated 6th February 2017</div><div class="PageHead__sponsor"><div><div data-ad-branding="one_square_meter" id="ad_mod_011ba0778"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="BasicArticle__hero BasicArticle__videoHero"><div class="BasicArticle__heroWrapper"><div class="VideoPlayer__component VideoPlayer__component"><div class="VideoPlayer__videoPlayerContainer"><div class="VideoPlayer__videoPlayer"><div id="heroVideoPlayer"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="SocialTimeBar__container"><div class="SocialTimeBar__component"><div class="SocialTimeBar__wrapper"><div class="SocialTimeBar__image"><div class="Image__component Image__hasAspectRatio" style="padding-top:100.00%"><img class="Image__image" src="https://dynaimage.cdn.cnn.com/cnn/e_blur:500,q_auto:low,w_50,c_fill,g_auto,h_50,ar_1:1/http%3A%2F%2Fcdn.cnn.com%2Fcnnnext%2Fdam%2Fassets%2F170125113315-shanghai-tower-art-space-super-tease.jpg"/></div></div><div class="SocialTimeBar__title">Shanghai Tower unveils world&#x27;s highest art space</div><div class="SocialBar__component SocialBar__isShare"><div class="SocialBar__links"><span class="SocialBar__link SocialBar__facebook"></span><span class="SocialBar__link SocialBar__twitter"></span><span class="SocialBar__link SocialBar__whatsapp"></span></div></div><div class="SocialTimeBar__bar" style="width:0%"></div></div></div></div><div class="Zone__component BasicArticle__zone"><div class="Zone__wrapper"><div class="BasicArticle__body"><div class="BasicArticle__main"><div class="BasicArticle__authors"><div class="BasicArticle__writers">Written by <span class="BasicArticle__writer">By Andrea Lo, CNN</span></div></div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__isDropCap">Ever since its completion last year, the Shanghai Tower has been the second tallest building on earth -- just behind the Burj Khalifa in Dubai. </div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">Soon it will have another accolade to its name. </div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">The 2,073 feet (632 meter) tall tower is opening the highest art space in the world. Located on the 126th floor of this 128-story building, it will feature an immersive auditory experience designed to serenade visitors to Shanghai.</div><div class="BasicArticle__ad BasicArticle__pad"><div class="Ad__component"><div id="ad_rect_atf_01" class="Ad__tag"></div></div></div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">Grammy-winning composer and producer Simon Franglen, who is behind famous theme songs from Hollywood blockbusters "Avatar" and "Titanic", was commissioned to create the symphony that will play in this venue.</div><div class="BasicArticle__embed BasicArticle__padLarge"><div class="HTMLEmbed__component"></div></div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad"><h3>Top of the world</h3></div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">So why a symphony for a skyscraper?</div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">The inspiration, it seems, was the view.</div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">"I have been at the top of many of the big buildings in the world, and this is something different," Franglen tells CNN. "(It is truly) like something from another world."</div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">From the top of the twisted tower, visitors have panoramic views of Shanghai, including its historic Bund waterfront area.</div><div class="BasicArticle__image BasicArticle__padLarge"><div><div class="Image__component"><img class="Image__image" src="https://dynaimage.cdn.cnn.com/cnn/e_blur:500,q_auto:low,w_50,c_fit/http%3A%2F%2Fcdn.cnn.com%2Fcnnnext%2Fdam%2Fassets%2F170125113315-shanghai-tower-art-space.jpg" alt=""/></div><div class="BasicArticle__caption"><span class="BasicArticle__credit">Connie Zhou</span></div></div></div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">Before starting work, the composer was asked to meet the directors at the tower, and explain his vision.</div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">"The way they were talking about the building and how the space works reminded me very much of the meridians and energy flows in acupuncture. I mentioned this, and I think that was part of the reason why they decided I understood what they were trying to do," he says. </div><div class="BasicArticle__embed BasicArticle__padLarge"><div class="HTMLEmbed__component"></div></div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad"><h3>A day in Shanghai</h3></div><div class="BasicArticle__ad BasicArticle__pad"><div class="Ad__component"><div id="ad_rect_btf_01" class="Ad__tag"></div></div></div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">After a walk in Shanghai Park, Franglen composed a piece based on a day in the city that also reflects the aesthetics of the tower. </div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad"><a href="http://edition.cnn.com/2016/10/05/asia/worlds-fastest-tower/">Skyscraper with a need for speed: China unveils world's fastest elevator</a></div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">"Shanghai ... is a city for the 22nd century," he says. "It feels 100 years ahead of everywhere else in the world.</div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">"When you look at the skyscraper, it doesn't look like any other skyscraper in the world. It looks like it grows from the ground, rather than being stamped on the ground like many skyscrapers do. I wanted to write a piece of music that felt like it grew."</div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">Franglen's symphony begins with bird song Franglen heard in the park, followed by the sound of the city waking up, with car horns, people rushing, and even an occasional bleep from a cell phone. This is followed by the sound of a river -- "I needed something that could flow through the piece of music" -- as well as of the tower's construction. </div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">It closes with sounds inspired by sunset. </div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad"><h3>Surround sound</h3></div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">Listening to Franglen's piece will be an all-consuming experience thanks to the 260 loudspeakers he has had installed in the space. </div><div class="BasicArticle__image BasicArticle__padLarge"><div><div class="Image__component"><img class="Image__image" src="https://dynaimage.cdn.cnn.com/cnn/e_blur:500,q_auto:low,w_50,c_fit/http%3A%2F%2Fcdn.cnn.com%2Fcnnnext%2Fdam%2Fassets%2F161201185645-shanghai-tower-art-space.png" alt="Inside the art space"/></div><div class="BasicArticle__caption">Inside the art space<!-- --> <span class="BasicArticle__credit"></span><span class="BasicArticle__credit"></span></div></div></div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">"They're above you, they're below you, they're everywhere," he says.</div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">"If I want to put (the sound of) a bell in front of your face, I can -- because we're using a unique sound system that allows me to put music in free space," he says, referring to the unusual aural experience created by strategic loudspeaker placement.</div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">"The sounds spin around in the space," he adds. "What I've done is written a piece of music that allows you to walk around inside it." </div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">The music was performed by four orchestras, comprising 240 players, and features a 48 voice-strong choir, 60 drums and 55 bells. The four orchestral parts interlock in a complex manner. </div><div class="BasicArticle__pullquote BasicArticle__pad"><div class="BasicArticle__pullquoteText">If I want to put (the sound of) a bell in front of your face, I can -- because we&#x27;re using a unique sound system</div><div class="BasicArticle__pullquoteAuthor">Simon Franglen, composer</div></div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">"One section of the orchestra would play one set of the notes, another set would play another -- and they would play against each other, so that they're almost competing in the three-dimensional space."</div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">Franglen says different versions of the piece, varying in length, will be played  in the space throughout the year. A six to seven minute-long version will be played to new visitors, to give them a sense of the experience, while a 20-minute composition is also in place for special events. </div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">The space will also feature a viewing gallery, where the building's tuned mass damper -- which stablizes the tower, and is normally hidden out of sight -- can be seen. </div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad"><h3>Cultural heart</h3></div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">Franglen calls the symphonic suite "one of the most exciting projects" he has ever worked on. </div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">The opening date of the art space and ticket prices are yet to be announced, but it is intended to be the heart of cultural happenings in the tower. </div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">"I hope that in the future other places build these types of installations and will realize culture is really important," he says.</div><div class="BasicArticle__paragraph BasicArticle__pad">"The work Shanghai Tower is trying to do, which is to think more than just in terms of commerce, is really special."</div><div class="BasicArticle__outbrainMain"><div class="BasicArticle__outbrain"><div class="OUTBRAIN" data-src="http://www.cnn.com/style/article/symphony-shanghai-tower/index.html" data-widget-id="AR_36" data-ob-template="cnn"></div></div><div class="BasicArticle__outbrain"><div class="OUTBRAIN" data-src="http://www.cnn.com/style/article/symphony-shanghai-tower/index.html" data-widget-id="AR_13" data-ob-template="cnn"></div></div></div></div><div
